"Hi,

Here's the code snippet showing the async calls I'm making:

```mercury
async function fetchData(url) {
  const response = await fetch(url);
  return await response.json();
}

const urls = [
  'https://api.example.com/data1',
  'https://api.example.com/data2',
  'https://api.example.com/data3'
];

async function main() {
  const results = await Promise.all(urls.map(fetchData));
  console.log(results);
}

main();
```

As you can see, I'm using `Promise.all` to handle the concurrent requests. However, the `results` array doesn't always reflect the order of the URLs in the `urls` array.

"Hi Aetheros Support,

I'm writing to suggest an improvement for the IAM service, specifically regarding role inheritance. Currently, we have situations where a child role inherits all permissions from the parent role, which isn't always ideal.

For instance, we might have a 'Developer' role that needs access to specific cloud resources for development purposes. We then have a 'Senior Developer' role that needs all the permissions of a 'Developer' but with additional access, say, to production logs.

With a more granular inheritance model, we could assign only the necessary permissions to the 'Developer' role and then selectively inherit and add permissions for the 'Senior Developer' role. This would significantly improve security and management within our organization.

Could you consider implementing a more fine-grained role inheritance feature in the IAM service?

Thanks,
John Doe"

"Hi Support Team,

* Code Snippet (simplified):

```mercury
// ... other code ...

let sharedResource = null;

concurrently {
  // Thread 1
  sharedResource = someFunction();
}
concurrently {
  // Thread 2
  print(sharedResource.toString()); // Potential NullPointerException here
}

// ... other code ...
```

* Concurrency Model: We are using the built-in `concurrently` block for managing threads.

As you can see, the issue arises because Thread 2 might try to access `sharedResource` before Thread 1 has finished initializing it, leading to the NullPointerException.

Any help with synchronizing access or other solutions would be greatly appreciated.
